**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Agentic Correctness: Implement Kubernetes Custom Resource Client

## Your Task

Write a Go file `crd_client.go` that implements a typed client for a custom resource `Widget` (group `example.com`, version `v1`). Your implementation must follow the patterns established in the Kubernetes client-go codebase: 1. Embed or use the `rest.Interface` client from `k8s.io/client-go/rest`. 2. Implement `Create`, `Get`, `List`, and `Delete` methods following the same parameter conventions as `k8s.io/client-go/kubernetes/typed/` clients. 3. Use proper `context.Context` propagation. Write your implementation to `/workspace/crd_client.go`. Also write `/workspace/answer.json` listing the client-go source files you referenced.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
*(none — all repos available locally)*

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?
- **Keyword presence**: Are required terms present in your explanation?

## Summary

I've implemented a typed client for the custom Kubernetes resource `Widget` (group: `example.com`, version: `v1`) following the established patterns in the Kubernetes client-go codebase.

### Files Created

**1. `/workspace/crd_client.go`** - Contains:
- `Widget`, `WidgetSpec`, `WidgetStatus`, and `WidgetList` types with proper metav1 struct tags
- `WidgetInterface` defining the API contract (Create, Get, List, Delete methods)
- `widgetClient` struct that embeds `rest.Interface` for HTTP communication
- Method implementations following the standard k8s.io/client-go parameter conventions:
  - `Create(ctx context.Context, widget *Widget, opts metav1.CreateOptions) (*Widget, error)`
  - `Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.GetOptions) (*Widget, error)`
  - `List(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (*WidgetList, error)`
  - `Delete(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.DeleteOptions) error`

### Implementation Details

The client uses the `rest.Interface` pattern with method chaining:
```go
c.client.Get().
    Prefix("apis", "example.com", "v1").
    Namespace(c.ns).
    Resource("widgets").
    Name(name).
    VersionedParams(&opts, ParameterCodec).
    Do(ctx).
    Into(result)
```

This approach:
- Properly propagates `context.Context` for timeout and cancellation
- Uses `rest.Request` methods for HTTP operations
- Leverages `Result.Into()` for response decoding and `Result.Error()` for error handling
- Follows the established Kubernetes API patterns

- Referenced source files from client-go (rest/client.go, rest/request.go, typed client examples, scale/client.go)
- Key symbols (Interface, Request, Result)

package main

import (
	"context"

	metav1 "k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1"
	"k8s.io/client-go/rest"
)

// Widget is a custom resource representing a widget
type Widget struct {
	metav1.TypeMeta   `json:",inline"`
	metav1.ObjectMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
	Spec              WidgetSpec   `json:"spec,omitempty"`
	Status            WidgetStatus `json:"status,omitempty"`
}

// WidgetSpec defines the desired state of a Widget
type WidgetSpec struct {
	Name string `json:"name,omitempty"`
}

// WidgetStatus defines the observed state of a Widget
type WidgetStatus struct {
	Phase string `json:"phase,omitempty"`
}

// WidgetList is a list of Widget resources
type WidgetList struct {
	metav1.TypeMeta `json:",inline"`
	metav1.ListMeta `json:"metadata,omitempty"`
	Items           []Widget `json:"items"`
}

// WidgetInterface defines the methods to work with Widget resources.
type WidgetInterface interface {
	Create(ctx context.Context, widget *Widget, opts metav1.CreateOptions) (*Widget, error)
	Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.GetOptions) (*Widget, error)
	List(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (*WidgetList, error)
	Delete(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.DeleteOptions) err
... (truncated)

The crd_client.go file implements a typed client for a custom resource Widget (group: example.com, version: v1) by embedding the rest.Interface client, following the pattern seen in scale/client.go. The implementation uses the rest.Request methods (Get, Post, Delete) that return *Request objects, which are then configured with namespace, resource, and name using method chaining (AbsPath, VersionedParams, Body), and finally executed with Do(ctx). Results are handled using the Result type's Into() and Error() methods. The custom types (Widget, WidgetList) implement the necessary metav1 interfaces for Kubernetes API objects. All methods properly propagate context.Co

// Create creates a new Widget resource.
// The returned Widget object will have the server-populated fields set.
func (c *widgetClient) Create(ctx context.Context, widget *Widget, opts metav1.CreateOptions) (*Widget, error) {
	result := &Widget{}
	err := c.client.
		Post().
		AbsPath("/apis/example.com/v1/namespaces", c.ns, "widgets").
		VersionedParams(&opts, ParameterCodec).
		Body(widget).
		Do(ctx).
		Into(result)
	return result, err
}

// Get retrieves a Widget resource by name.
func (c *widgetClient) Get(ctx context.Context, name string, opts metav1.GetOptions) (*Widget, error) {
	result := &Widget{}
	err := c.client.
		Get().
		AbsPath("/apis/example.com/v1/namespaces", c.ns, "widgets", name).
		VersionedParams(&opts, ParameterCodec).
		Do(ctx).
		Into(result)
	return result, err
}

// List retrieves all Widget resources in the namespace.
func (c *widgetClient) List(ctx context.Context, opts metav1.ListOptions) (*WidgetList, error) {
	result := &WidgetList{}
	err := c.client.
		Get().
		AbsPath("/apis/example.com/v1/namespaces", c.ns, "widgets").
		VersionedParams(&opts, ParameterCodec).
